| 1:02:42| Whereas, according to the Center of Disease and Prevention, CDC, breast cancer is the second most common cancer among women in the United States| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3762)|
| 1:02:49| and is expected to be diagnosed in 281,550 women in the United States in 2021.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3769)|
| 1:02:57| Whereas, increasing the public's knowledge about the importance of early detection of breast cancer diagnosis and treatment can save lives.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3777)|
| 1:03:04| Whereas, Breast Cancer Awareness Month is a worldwide annual campaign in October to highlight the importance of breast cancer awareness, education, and research| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3784)|
| 1:03:14| and to promote mammography as the most effective weapon in the fight against breast cancer.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3794)|
| 1:03:20| And whereas the efforts of various organizations have made a major contribution to spreading breast cancer awareness through outreach, education, and screening programs| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3800)|
| 1:03:30| and have empowered women with the life-saving message of early detection and the importance of having regular mammograms.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3810)|
| 1:03:38| Whereas, one such organization that is dedicated to the fight against cancer is the American Cancer Society, located both nationwide and in Knoxville.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3818)|
| 1:03:46| Whereas, the commission wishes to acknowledge and commend the extraordinary commitment and effort invested in this cause by the American Cancer Society| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3826)|
| 1:03:54| and the other organizations in our community who are working towards a cure and to raise awareness.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3834)|
| 1:03:59| Whereas, Breast Cancer Awareness Month is an opportunity to unite all citizens in our community to show their support for everyone affected by breast cancer| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3839)|
| 1:04:07| and to help prevent breast cancer deaths through increased education and regular screening tests.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3847)|
| 1:04:12| Now therefore, be it resolved by the commission of Knox County as follows.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=3852)|

| 1:08:17| Our engine companies responded to 808 medical first responder calls, 77 car crashes, 22 residential structure fires, 72 false alarms,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4097)|

| 1:08:40| It's for a total of 1,430 for the month of September.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4120)|
| 1:08:45| We responded to properties valued at $300,340 and had a property loss of $147,000,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4125)|
| 1:08:53| which means we saved an average of 51% of the valued property with an average response time of 4 minutes and 20 seconds.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4133)|

| 1:10:11| So Madison is a young lady that, like most of us, headed off to work on April the 15th of this year,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4211)|
| 1:10:17| but on this day, Madison's life would change forever.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4217)|

| 1:10:43| I'll get them straight in a minute, began treating Madison.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4243)|
| 1:10:48| Her left leg was bleeding profusely.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4248)|
| 1:10:50| We did not bring pictures, I promise.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4250)|
| 1:10:52| I wanted to keep it all clean.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4252)|
| 1:10:54| Her left leg was bleeding profusely and barely attached to her body.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4254)|
| 1:11:00| Our fire medics administered fluids and new medication that enhances the body's ability for blood to clot, thus slowing the bleeding.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4260)|

| 1:11:13| well within the golden hour for trauma care.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-211025?start=4273)|
